\DoxyCodeLine{01041\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ calcLightEff(\textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ *lightEff,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ lai,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ par)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01042\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01043\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Information\ on\ the\ distribution\ of\ LAI\ with\ height\ is\ available}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01044\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ as\ of\ March\ 2007\ ...\ contact\ Dr.\ Maggie\ Prater\ Maggie.Prater@colorado.edu}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01045\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01046\ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{static}\ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ NUM\_LAYERS\ =\ 6;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01047\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ believe\ it\ or\ not,\ 6\ layers\ gives\ approximately\ the\ same\ result\ as\ 100}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01048\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ layers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01049\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01050\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ layer;\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ counter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01051\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ cumLai;\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ lai\ from\ this\ layer\ up}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01052\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ lightIntensity;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01053\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ currLightEff\ =\ 0.0,\ cumLightEff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01054\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ currfAPAR\ =\ 0.0,\ cumfAPAR;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01055\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ coeff;\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ current\ coefficient\ in\ Simpson's\ rule}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01056\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01057\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (lai\ >\ 0\ \&\&\ par\ >\ 0)\ \{\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ must\ have\ at\ least\ some\ leaves\ and\ some\ light}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01058\ \ \ \ \ cumLightEff\ =\ 0.0;\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ running\ sum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01059\ \ \ \ \ layer\ =\ 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01060\ \ \ \ \ coeff\ =\ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01061\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ err;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01062\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ fAPAR;\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Calculation\ of\ fAPAR\ according\ to\ 1\ -\/\ exp(attenuation*LAI)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01063\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ double\ APAR;\ \ \ \ //\ Absorbed\ PAR\ by\ the\ canopy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01064\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ double\ lightIntensityTop,\ lightIntensityBottom;\ \ //\ PAR\ absorbed\ by\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01065\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ canopy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01066\ \ \ \ \ cumfAPAR\ =\ 0.0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01067\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01068\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}\ (layer\ <=\ NUM\_LAYERS)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01069\ \ \ \ \ \ \ cumLai\ =\ lai\ *\ ((double)layer\ /\ NUM\_LAYERS);\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ lai\ from\ this\ layer\ up}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01070\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ (starting\ at\ top)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01071\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01072\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ between\ 0\ and\ par}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01073\ \ \ \ \ \ \ lightIntensity\ =\ par\ *\ exp(-\/1.0\ *\ params.attenuation\ *\ cumLai);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01074\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01075\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ between\ 0\ and\ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01076\ \ \ \ \ \ \ currLightEff\ =\ (1\ -\/\ pow(2,\ (-\/1.0\ *\ lightIntensity\ /\ params.halfSatPar)));}
\DoxyCodeLine{01077\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01078\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ when\ lightIntensity\ =\ halfSatPar,\ currLightEff\ =\ 1/2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01079\ \ \ \ \ \ \ cumLightEff\ +=\ coeff\ *\ currLightEff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01080\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01081\ \ \ \ \ \ \ currfAPAR\ =\ 1\ -\/\ (lightIntensity\ /\ par);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01082\ \ \ \ \ \ \ cumfAPAR\ +=\ coeff\ *\ currfAPAR;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01083\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01084\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ now\ move\ to\ the\ next\ layer:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01085\ \ \ \ \ \ \ layer++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01086\ \ \ \ \ \ \ coeff\ =\ 2\ *\ (1\ +\ layer\ \%\ 2);\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ coeff.\ goes\ 1,\ 4,\ 2,\ 4,\ ...,\ 2,\ 4,\ 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01087\ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01088\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ last\ value\ should\ have\ had\ a\ coefficient\ of\ 1,\ but\ actually\ had\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01089\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ coefficient\ of\ 2,\ so\ subtract\ 1:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01090\ \ \ \ \ cumLightEff\ -\/=\ currLightEff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01091\ \ \ \ \ *lightEff\ =\ cumLightEff\ /\ (3.0\ *\ NUM\_LAYERS);\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ multiplying\ by\ (h/3)\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01092\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Simpson's\ rule}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01093\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01094\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ now\ calculate\ fAPAR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01095\ \ \ \ \ cumfAPAR\ -\/=\ currfAPAR;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01096\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ average\ value,\ multiplying\ by\ h/3\ in\ Simpson's\ rule,\ and\ dividing\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01097\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ number\ of\ steps}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01098\ \ \ \ \ fAPAR\ =\ cumfAPAR\ /\ (3.0\ *\ NUM\_LAYERS);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01099\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01100\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ lightIntensityTop\ =\ par;\ \ //\ Energy\ at\ the\ top\ of\ the\ canopy}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02523\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ EVENT\_HANDLER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02524\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ processEvents(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void})\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02525\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ should\ be\ in\ events.h/c,\ but\ with\ all\ the\ global\ state\ defined\ in\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02526\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ file,\ let's\ leave\ it\ here\ for\ now.\ Maybe\ someday\ we\ will\ factor\ that\ out.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02527\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02528\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ If\ locEvent\ starts\ off\ NULL,\ this\ function\ will\ just\ fall\ through,\ as\ it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02529\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ should.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02530\ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ climYear\ =\ climate-\/>year;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02531\ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ climDay\ =\ climate-\/>day;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02532\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02533\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ events\ file\ has\ been\ tested\ on\ read,\ so\ we\ know\ this\ event\ list\ should}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02534\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ be\ in\ chrono\ order.\ However,\ we\ need\ to\ check\ to\ make\ sure\ the\ current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02535\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ event\ is\ not\ in\ the\ past,\ as\ that\ would\ indicate\ an\ event\ that\ did\ not\ have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02536\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ a\ corresponding\ climate\ file\ record.}}
